function create_ezolpl(pvID, rv) {

    var d = new Date();

    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));

    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();

    __ez.ck.setByCat("ezux_lpl_314288=" + new Date().getTime() + "|" + pvID + "|" + rv + "; " + expires, 3);

}

function attach_ezolpl(pvID, rv) {

    if (document.readyState === "complete") {

        create_ezolpl(pvID, rv);

    }

    if(window.attachEvent) {

        window.attachEvent("onload", create_ezolpl, pvID, rv);

    } else {

        if(window.onload) {

            var curronload = window.onload;

            var newonload = function(evt) {

                curronload(evt);

                create_ezolpl(pvID, rv);

            };

            window.onload = newonload;

        } else {

            window.onload = create_ezolpl.bind(null, pvID, rv);

        }

    }

}



__ez.queue.addFunc("attach_ezolpl", "attach_ezolpl", ["71ce34e9-5acc-4f40-5544-8c2bcc2c39f8", "false"], false, ['/detroitchicago/boise.js'], true, false, false, false);

</script>

                 </div>

                 <h2 style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">How to Automate 'Practice Form' with Selenium WebDriver</h2>

                 <div>

                  <br>

                 </div>

                 <div>

                  <span style="color: #303030;">This is a demo web form which contains all the form elements which are mostly present on any web page. So, by automating this form you would learn all the WebDriver commands which are required to automate a web page. </span>This web from contains following web elements:

                 </div>

                 <div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">

                  <ul>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Links</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Text boxes</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Radio buttons</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Date Picker</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Check boxes</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select box</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Multi Select box</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Upload Image button</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Download link</span></span></li>

                  </ul>

                 </div>

                 <div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">

                  <span style="color: #303030;"><span><b>Steps to Automate:</b></span></span>

                 </div>

                 <div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">

                  <ol>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Open this link - https://www.techlistic.com/p/selenium-practice-form.html</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Enter first and last name (textbox).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select gender (radio button).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select years of experience (radio button).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Enter date.</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select Profession (Checkbox).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select Automation tools you are familiar with (multiple checkboxes).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select Continent (Select box).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Select multiple commands from a multi select box.</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>If you can handle Upload image then try it or leave this step.</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Click on Download file link and handle the download file pop-up (leave it if you are beginner).</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Click on Submit button.</span></span></li>

                   <li><span style="color: #303030;"><span>Try your own logic and automate it without any help. If you still find it difficult to automate then follow reference links. </span></span></li>

                  </ol>

                  <div>

                   <span style="font-size: 14px;"><b><br></b></span>

                  </div>

                  <div>

                   <span style="font-size: 14px;"><b>Example Code:</b></span>

                  </div>

                  <div>

                   <span style="font-size: 14px;"><b><br></b></span>

                  </div>

                  <div>

                   <div style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-color: gray; border-image: initial; border-style: solid; border-width: 0.1em 0.1em 0.1em 0.8em; color: #333333; font-family: Verdana, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; overflow: auto; padding: 0.2em 0.6em; width: auto;">

                    <pre style="line-height: 16.25px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-top: 0px;"><span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">package</span> com.<span style="color: #0000cc;">techlistic</span>.<span style="color: #0000cc;">tute</span>;



<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.By</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.WebDriver</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.chrome.ChromeDriver</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.remote.DesiredCapabilities</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.Dimension</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.WebElement</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.interactions.Actions</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.ExpectedConditions</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.WebDriverWait</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.JavascriptExecutor</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.Alert</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">org.openqa.selenium.Keys</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">java.util.*</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">java.net.MalformedURLException</span>;

<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">import</span> <span style="color: #0e84b5; font-weight: bold;">java.net.URL</span>;



<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">public</span> <span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">class</span> <span style="color: #bb0066; font-weight: bold;">PracticeFormTest</span> {



    <span style="color: #888888;">// Main Method is the execution point of any Java Program</span>

    <span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">public</span> <span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">static</span> <span style="color: #333399; font-weight: bold;">void</span> <span style="color: #0066bb; font-weight: bold;">main</span>(String[] args){

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Initialize Webdriver Object</span>

        System.<span style="color: #0000cc;">setProperty</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"webdriver.chrome.driver"</span>, <span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"D:\\chromedriver.exe"</span>);

        WebDriver driver = <span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">new</span> ChromeDriver();

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Open URL</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">get</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"https://www.techlistic.com/p/selenium-practice-form.html"</span>);

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Set Chrome window size</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">manage</span>().<span style="color: #0000cc;">window</span>().<span style="color: #0000cc;">setSize</span>(<span style="color: #008800; font-weight: bold;">new</span> Dimension(<span style="color: #0000dd; font-weight: bold;">1552</span>, <span style="color: #0000dd; font-weight: bold;">840</span>));

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Enter Firstname</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">name</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"firstname"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">name</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"firstname"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">sendKeys</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"Tom"</span>);

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Set Lastname</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">name</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"lastname"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">name</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"lastname"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">sendKeys</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"Wood"</span>);

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Gender</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"sex-0"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Experience</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"exp-4"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Enter Date</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"datepicker"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"datepicker"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">sendKeys</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"16-10-2020"</span>);

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Profession</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"profession-1"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Automation Tool</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"tool-2"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();



        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Continent</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"continents"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

        WebElement dropdown = driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"continents"</span>));

        dropdown.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">xpath</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"//option[. = 'Europe']"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();



        <span style="color: #888888;">// Select Command</span>

        WebElement dropdown = driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"selenium_commands"</span>));

        dropdown.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">xpath</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"//option[. = 'Browser Commands']"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();



        <span style="color: #888888;">// Scroll Vertical</span>

        js.<span style="color: #0000cc;">executeScript</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"window.scrollTo(0,675.5555419921875)"</span>);



        <span style="color: #888888;">// Click Submit</span>

        driver.<span style="color: #0000cc;">findElement</span>(By.<span style="color: #0000cc;">id</span>(<span style="background-color: #fff0f0;">"submit"</span>)).<span style="color: #0000cc;">click</span>();

  }

}</pre>

                   </div>

                  </div>

                  <div>

                   <br>

                  </div>

                  <div>

                   <br>

                  </div>

                 </div>

            <h3 class="post-title"><a href="https://www.techlistic.com/2020/07/automation-testing-demo-websites.html">10+ Best Demo Websites for Selenium Automation Testing Practice</a></h3> 

            <div class="post-header"> 

             <div class="post-header-line-1"> 

             </div> 

            </div> 

            <div class="item-content float-container"> 

             <div class="item-thumbnail"> <a href="https://www.techlistic.com/2020/07/automation-testing-demo-websites.html"> <img alt="Image" sizes="72px" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20width%3D%22316%22%20height%3D%22210%22%3E%3C%2Fsvg%3E" data-ezsrcset="https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDp0nlW3V8fi_VSf9OJea3wrySTfF9Da6DNsnWz4uLM4BWXhQdBBOtYaTvVqGYty0GquKVfFSHOSx0guodNzqGQA2_qLEGV1c9V6gsrCeMo62KmJSNpVcWRKOEiM0BhUxL4mj3LM1knFCIG_RY3nbfOhem0o9MuHvyI0cKgcPXn0b3yLoSn9CHY6OQsQ=w72-h72-p-k-no-nu 72w,https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDp0nlW3V8fi_VSf9OJea3wrySTfF9Da6DNsnWz4uLM4BWXhQdBBOtYaTvVqGYty0GquKVfFSHOSx0guodNzqGQA2_qLEGV1c9V6gsrCeMo62KmJSNpVcWRKOEiM0BhUxL4mj3LM1knFCIG_RY3nbfOhem0o9MuHvyI0cKgcPXn0b3yLoSn9CHY6OQsQ=w144-h144-p-k-no-nu 144w" ezimgfmt="rs rscb1 src ng ngcb1 srcset" class="ezlazyload" data-ezsrc="https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDp0nlW3V8fi_VSf9OJea3wrySTfF9Da6DNsnWz4uLM4BWXhQdBBOtYaTvVqGYty0GquKVfFSHOSx0guodNzqGQA2_qLEGV1c9V6gsrCeMo62KmJSNpVcWRKOEiM0BhUxL4mj3LM1knFCIG_RY3nbfOhem0o9MuHvyI0cKgcPXn0b3yLoSn9CHY6OQsQ=w327-h210"> </a>

             <div class="popular-posts-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container"> 

              <div class="snippet-item r-snippetized">

                We certainly need demo websites for various purposes, like learning new tools and for automation testing practice. In this post, we cherry picked some of the best websites to practice Selenium automation testing. These set of demo websites would help you to enhance your automation skills.  This dummy websites post can help various people like,  Automation Testing learners, Experienced professionals and even Automation Testing tutors/teachers. They all can benefit from these demo websites. In this post, you won't only get the links of the demo website but alongside get the practice exercises links for automation practice. Table of Content 1. Techlistic Automation Practice Form 2. Amazon like Demo E-Commerce Website 3. Make My Trip like Travel Portal 4. Demo Automation Practice Web Table 5. Google.com 6. Demo Website for Handling Alerts 7. Way2Automation Demo 8. NewTours DemoAUT 9. The Demo Site 10. DemoQA BONUS - Demo Websites for API Testing 11. Restful Booker 12. Pet Store Let

            <h3 class="post-title"><a href="https://www.techlistic.com/2020/06/automate-ecommerce-website.html">Automate Amazon like E-Commerce Website with Selenium WebDriver</a></h3> 

            <div class="post-header"> 

             <div class="post-header-line-1"> 

             </div> 

            </div> 

            <div class="item-content float-container"> 

             <div class="item-thumbnail"> <a href="https://www.techlistic.com/2020/06/automate-ecommerce-website.html"> <img alt="Image" sizes="72px" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20width%3D%22127%22%20height%3D%2288%22%3E%3C%2Fsvg%3E" data-ezsrcset="https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/1.bp.blogspot.com/-pxNB8-NP0-I/V3IpyJWQAnI/AAAAAAAABtw/urrHJ_94E5QvvJbD310TOS7qQsaQkwG9ACPcBGAYYCw/w72-h72-p-k-no-nu/Web.jpg 72w,https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/1.bp.blogspot.com/-pxNB8-NP0-I/V3IpyJWQAnI/AAAAAAAABtw/urrHJ_94E5QvvJbD310TOS7qQsaQkwG9ACPcBGAYYCw/w144-h144-p-k-no-nu/Web.jpg 144w" ezimgfmt="rs rscb1 src ng ngcb1 srcset" class="ezlazyload" data-ezsrc="https://www.techlistic.com/ezoimgfmt/1.bp.blogspot.com/-pxNB8-NP0-I/V3IpyJWQAnI/AAAAAAAABtw/urrHJ_94E5QvvJbD310TOS7qQsaQkwG9ACPcBGAYYCw/w200-h88/Web.jpg"> </a> 

             </div> 

             <div class="popular-posts-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container"> 

              <div class="snippet-item r-snippetized">

                We have created this post as a 'Self Learning Project Assignment' for the automation geeks. In this project assignment, you will learn to automate different functionalities of an e-commerce website.  This assignment is rated as 'Pro' level, which means you should have sound knowledge of all the Selenium concepts. We'll create test plan and then automate an e-commerce website which is quite similar to amazon.com. Table of Content 1. What should you know before starting this Project assignment? 2. Which functionalities will we automate in this Project assignment? 3. Create Test Plan for Amazon like e-commerce website 4. Automate Amazon like e-commerce website: Automate User Registration and Login of e-commerce website Automate Search feature of e-commerce website Automate "Buy Product" feature of e-Commerce website 1. What should you know before starting this project assignment? You should know following topics, before start

             <div class="popular-posts-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container"> 

              <div class="snippet-item r-snippetized">

                As an Automation Tester you get to play with links present on the website. Links are one of the most important part of the webpage. So, it's always important to not leave any broken link on any website. Testing the links manually could be a tough and time taking task. In this post, we'll learn to automate the URL links testing. 1. What is a Broken Link? A broken link is a URL which is not working or not reachable. There are multiple reasons for it's dis-functioning. There are different http error status codes which the browser shows when the link is broken. These error codes have different meanings. Let's take a look at the different http status codes. 200 - It means success, link is working. 404 - It's the most common one, which mean Page not found. 403 - Authorization is required to access the page.  400 - It has different meanings, bad request, bad host, timeout etc. 500 - Internal server error. 2. Why a link broke? A link might not be working due to many reason
